Install 35 linear feet of drain tile to prevent water seepage under the door. This work will include trenching at the proper slope, laying perforated pipe on a gravel base, and covering it with additional gravel and landscape fabric. The trench will be backfilled and leveled to restore the area. This drainage system is designed to effectively redirect water away from the door, eliminating future seepage issues.
